     - Topic: Learner feedback after a course session
     - Question number: 8
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.

Then, the user will ask to convert it into a specified format.

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Learner feedback after a course session with 8 questions

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a set of eight engaging questions that can be used in a learner feedback survey:
1. "On a scale from 1-5, how would you rate the overall quality of this course?" This question will help determine if learners felt like they were able to get something valuable out of their time spent on the class and whether or not it met expectations for them in terms of content delivery style etcetera.
2. "What did you enjoy most about taking part in our session? Please provide specific examples." This question allows participants an opportunity to share what aspects they appreciated, which can be used as positive reinforcement when highlighting strengths within the course design or teaching methods employed by instructors involved with future iterations of this class if necessary.
3a/b: "If you could change one thing about our session format (either content OR delivery), what would it be? And why?" These two questions together allow learners to express any concerns they may have had regarding the course, providing valuable insight into areas where improvements can potentially make a significant difference in learner satisfaction and retention rates.
4. "How well did you feel that our learning objectives aligned with your personal goals for this session? Please explain." This question will help determine if learners felt like their needs were being met during the course, which is crucial to ensure maximum engagement from participants who might otherwise disengage due to misalignment between individual and group ambitions.
5a/b: "Did you feel comfortable asking questions or participating in discussions? If not, why?" These two linked but separate enquiries aim at understanding if learners felt encouraged enough throughout the session so that they could actively participate without fear of judgment; this information can be used to improve communication strategies and create a more inclusive environment for all attendees.
6: "How would you rate your engagement level with our course material? Were there any topics or activities where deeper exploration was desired?" This question allows participants an opportunity not only to express their overall satisfaction but also pinpoint specific areas of improvement, which can then be prioritized based on feedback received from multiple learners.
7: "How clear were the instructions given for each activity and assessment? Please provide examples." The seventh query focuses explicitly on clarity - a vital component in any educational setting; by asking participants to rate their understanding about specific instances within course materials, it becomes possible to identify potential pain points affecting learner success rates negatively.
8: "Do you have suggestions regarding how we can make our content more accessible or user-friendly? If yes then please specify." The last question encourages learners' active involvement in shaping future iterations of the course by asking them directly if they perceive any barriers to accessibility, allowing for targeted improvements based on firsthand experience rather than assumptions.
Please let me know which format you would like this converted into!

2. How well do you feel that the learning objectives were met throughout the duration of the course? Were there certain topics where more time should have been spent to help students better understand them, in retrospect? (Multiple choice: Strongly agree/Somewhat Agree /Neutral/Disagree/Strongly Disagree)
3. How would you rate your engagement with this particular course on a scale of 1-5 and provide any specific examples or anecdotes that come to mind when thinking about the level? (Multiple choice: Strongly agree, Somewhat Agree /Neutral/Disagree/Strongly Disagree)
4. Were there certain activities in this course which stood out as particularly effective for your learning and understanding of a topic or concept - if so please specify them below! Or were they less useful? (Multiple choice: Strongly agree, Somewhat Agree /Neutral/Disagree/Strongly Disagree)
5. Is there anything else you would like to share about this course that could help us improve it for future students or make the experience better overall - if so please specify below! Thank You!!

[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.

Generate me a questionnaire on Access to Technology and Tools with 9 questions

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a set of nine engaging questions about access to technology and tools:

1) How would you rate your overall level of agreement that all employees have equal access to necessary technologies and tools? (Strongly agree, somewhat agree, neutral, strongly disagree, or very strong disagreement?) Can we do better in this area as a company? Please elaborate.
2) In the past 6 months, how often did you feel like your work was limited by lack of technology/tools access compared to others and not because it wasn't available for everyone else too (Never / Rarely / Occasionally / Frequently or Always)? Can we do better in this area as a company?
3) How many devices, software licenses OR subscriptions does an average employee need at your organization on annual basis. Please specify the number and type of technology/tools required for each position (Less than 5; Between five to ten / More then Ten). Is there any room or necessity in reducing this count through better management?
4) Do you think that all employees have access to tools which are necessary, irrespective if they work remotely OR at the office. Can we do a Better job here as an organization (Yes/No)? If not why and what can be done about it specifically for your department or team in terms of technology?
5) How often does equipment failure affect you personally while working with others on same project, irrespective if they are remote OR at the office. Can we do a better job here as an organization (Yes/No)? If not why and what can be done about it specifically for your department or team in terms of technology?
6) How often have YOU PERSONALLY felt that you didn't get access to tools which would make YOUR work easier, more efficient OR productive. Can we do a better job here as an organization (Yes/No)? If not why and what can be done about it specifically for your position in terms of technology?
7) How often have YOU PERSONALLY felt that you didn't get access to tools which would make YOUR work easier, more efficient OR productive because the budget was already spent or there wasnâ€™t enough money. Can we do a better job here as an organization (Yes/No)? If not why and what can be done about it specifically for your position in terms of technology?
8) How often have YOU PERSONALLY felt that you didn't get access to tools which would make YOUR work easier, more efficient OR productive because the tool or software was too complicated. Can we do a better job here as an organization (Yes/No)? If not why and what can be done about it specifically for your position in terms of technology?
9) How often have YOU PERSONALLY felt that you didn't get access to tools which would make YOUR work easier, more efficient OR productive because the tool or software was NOT available. Can we do a better job here as an organization (Yes/No)? If not why and what can be done about it specifically for your position in terms of technology?

+---------------------[Questionnaire format] --------------------+

8. I am satisfied with how much time off and vacation days are granted to me, as per benefits policy? (Time Off Satisfaction.)

3) Do you think that it is important for people in leadership positions (managers/team leaders etc.) should give regular performance-related positive reinforcement to their subordinates, even if there are no negative things they need to address with them at the time? 4) Have you ever received feedback that was not actionable or specific enough for improvement in your opinion and how did it make YOU feel about receiving this type of vague information again, even if positive (options: Happy/Neutral / Unhappy)? Please explain why. [Can be more than one answer]

7) Have you ever given feedback to someone in leadership position about how things are going and what could potentially improve? And do these need a specific agenda for them, even if they're not related directly towards your performance but the team/department as whole (options: Yes / No). Please explain why.

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a set of seven engaging questions about workload management:
1) On average, how many hours do you spend each week working? * Examine whether this number feels manageable or overwhelming to the respondent. If it's too high and causing burnout, consider implementing time-management strategies like setting boundaries on when they are available for certain tasks/projects.* 2) How often does your workload feel unmanageable due to conflicting priorities? * This question can help identify if there is a need for better communication or prioritization of responsibilities. If the answer indicates frequent conflicts, consider implementing tools and techniques that allow team members to manage their own time more efficiently.* 3) Do you have enough resources (people/tools etc.) at your disposal? * This question can help uncover if there is a need for additional support or technology in order to better handle workload. If the answer indicates lack of necessary tools, consider investing into them and providing proper training on how they should be used.* 4) How frequently do you feel overloaded with tasks that are not part of your main responsibilities? * This question can help uncover if there is a need for delegation or redistribution. If the answer indicates frequent occurrence then it might mean some people have been given too many different things to handle and they should be reassigned.* 5) Do you feel like certain tasks are being pushed onto your plate because others don't want responsibility? * This question can help uncover if there is a need for better accountability. If the answer indicates that this happens often, consider implementing an effective system of task distribution where everyone feels comfortable with their responsibilities.* 6) How well do you feel like workload management tools are being utilized within your organization (either by yourself or others)? * This question can help uncover if there is a need for better training on how to use these resources. If the answer indicates that they aren't used properly, consider providing more information about them and encouraging their usage.* 7) How often do you feel like workload management tools are being misused within your organization? * This question can help uncover if there is a need for better communication or understanding of these resources. If the answer indicates that they aren't used properly, consider providing more information about them and encouraging their usage.*
Please let me know which format you would like this set in!

4) Is management approach to employee development consistent with company values and goals OR does it feel like something that needs improvement ? 5. How does your company handle conflicts among team members, especially when it comes between two people who have different opinions about how things should be done or handled internally?
8) Finally - do you think new employees are welcomed warmly and integrated into teams quickly enough so that they can contribute fully towards organizational success ? Or is there still room for improvement in this area too, making onboarding process smoother & more inclusive experience overall.

(Question type : Rating Scale + Textual Follow Up Questions to get more details about any specific incident if rating is less than 5/10). 4) Suppose that you are given an opportunity of working in a different shift, how likely will be able and willing for this change? Please elaborate on reasons behind your answer including impact it may have other team members or overall productivity if any! (Question Type: Likelihood Scale ) 5) If there was one thing which could magically transform the current workplace environment into perfect then what that would be ? Justify why you think so !( Question type : Open Ended / Multiple Choice ).
Please let me know how this set of questions looks and if any changes are needed. I am also able to convert these questionnaires in various formats like PDF, Word or even a chatbot conversation style for better user experience!

-------------------
[TEST] QUESTIONNAIRE_ID: 500100065
     - Topic: Workplace Environment
     - Question number: 7
-------------------
[PROMPTS]
     - System: 
You are a Questionnaire Generator that helps HR users investigate phenomena within the company.
Firstly, the user will ask you to generate a questionnaire specifying the topic and the number of questions.
Then, the user will ask to convert it into a specified format.
Be creative and vary the syntax of your questions to enhance user engagement. 

     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Workplace Environment with 7 questions

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a set of seven engaging and interactive questions about workplace environment:
1) On a scale from 1-5, how would you rate our current office space in terms of comfort? (Consider factors such as temperature, noise level, lighting etc.) Please provide specific examples to support your rating. For example - "I give it a score of 3 because the chairs are not comfortable enough for long hours."
2) If given an option between open and closed workspaces which one would you prefer? And why do think that is better than other type, in terms of productivity or comfort level etc., if possible please provide examples. For example - "I will choose a quiet space with four walls because I get easily distracted by noise."
3) How often are your meetings and discussions interrupted due to poor acoustics? And how does it affect the quality/quantity of work you produce in that time period, if possible please provide examples. For example - "I have faced interruptions at least 5 times a week because I can hear other people's conversations."
4) How frequently do your ideas and thoughts get lost due to poor layout or design? And how does it affect the quality/quantity of work you produce in that time period, if possible please provide examples. For example - "I have trouble finding space for my things because there is not enough storage area" on a scale from 1-5 where would rate our current office environment and why ?
5) If given an option to choose between different types of workspaces based upon your personality type, which one you will prefer? And please provide reasons. For example - "I am more productive in open spaces because I like interacting with people" or if possible give a rating out 1-7 on how much do we incorporate the concept into our office design and why ?
6) How important is it for your work environment to be aesthetically pleasing? And please provide examples. For example - "I think that an appealing workspace can increase my motivation" or if possible give a rating out 1-5 on how much do we incorporate the concept into our office design and why ?
7) How often have you felt uncomfortable in your current work environment due to poor ergonomics? And please provide examples. For example - "I feel pain because of my chair, it's not adjustable" or if possible give a rating out 1-5 on how much do we incorporate the concept into our office design and why ?

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure! Here is a set of seven engaging and interactive questions about workplace environment:
1) On a scale from 1-5, how would you rate our current office space in terms of comfort? (Consider factors such as temperature, noise level, lighting etc.) Please provide specific examples to support your rating. For example - "I give it a score of 3 because the chairs are not comfortable enough for long hours."
2) If given an option between open and closed workspaces which one would you prefer? And why do think that is better than other type, in terms of productivity or comfort level etc., if possible please provide examples. For example - "I will choose a quiet space with four walls because I get easily distracted by noise."
3) How often are your meetings and discussions interrupted due to poor acoustics? And how does it affect the quality/quantity of work you produce in that time period, if possible please provide examples. For example - "I have faced interruptions at least 5 times a week because I can hear other people's conversations."
4) How frequently do your ideas and thoughts get lost due to poor layout or design? And how does it affect the quality/quantity of work you produce in that time period, if possible please provide examples. For example - "I have trouble finding space for my things because there is not enough storage area" on a scale from 1-5 where would rate our current office environment and why ?
5) If given an option to choose between different types of workspaces based upon your personality type, which one you will prefer? And please provide reasons. For example - "I am more productive in open spaces because I like interacting with people" or if possible give a rating out 1-7 on how much do we incorporate the concept into our office design and why ?
6) How important is it for your work environment to be aesthetically pleasing? And please provide examples. For example - "I think that an appealing workspace can increase my motivation" or if possible give a rating out 1-5 on how much do we incorporate the concept into our office design and why ?
7) How often have you felt uncomfortable in your current work environment due to poor ergonomics? And please provide examples. For example - "I feel pain because of my chair, it's not adjustable" or if possible give a rating out 1-5 on how much do we incorporate the concept into our office design and why ?
Please let me know If you want any changes in questions above!
